[ 5832s]     def _RLSortRoots(roots):
[ 5832s]         """Sort the roots from _RLFindRoots, so that the root
[ 5832s]         locus doesn't show weird pseudo-branches as roots jump from
[ 5832s]         one branch to another."""
[ 5832s]     
[ 5832s]         sorted = zeros_like(roots)

[ 5832s]             if n == 0:
[ 5832s]                 sorted[n, :] = row
[ 5832s]             else:
